4a1(9): lha mo gsal khyab ma la phyag 'tshal lo// dbyengs kyi lha mo kun shes ma la phyag 'tshal lo// dbyings kyi lha m don grub ma la phyag 'tshal lo// dbyengs kyi lha

4b3(9): lo// dbyings kyi lha mo don gyi dbyings grub ma la phyag 'tshal lo// mkha' yi lha mo nam mkha' mtha' yas ma la phyag 'tshal lo// mkha' yi lha mo gsal ba mtha'

5a1(9): y/ 'tshal lo// mkha' yi lha mo 'jig rten gtos mkhyen ma la phyag 'tshal lo// mkha' yi lha mo sred pa'i rtsis mkhyen ma la phyag 'tshal lo// mkha' yi /
